# §5 Миллионер Reconciliation — Income-Floor Table per Archetype × Phase × Pricing-Tier

> **Cell C-06 | philosophy-expert | mode: critic**
>
> This section resolves the apparent contradiction among audio_529 ($1M+ миллионер framing),
> audio_470 ($20-50K/mo client bracket), and audio_452 (€150/hr × 4 hours = €600 operational
> cashflow). The three numbers operate on different units of analysis and are NOT comparable-in-kind.
> The resolution is epistemic, not diplomatic: each claim is grounded, scoped, and falsified per
> Popper P1; the income-floor table follows as a logical consequence.


## §5.0 Framing — the tension as an epistemic object

The apparent contradiction is not a contradiction. It is an instance of **AP-PHIL-2 (paradigm
conflation)** — three claims from different epistemic registers being read as if they occupy
the same unit-of-analysis space. They do not. [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]

Before any reconciliation, the three claims must be disaggregated as epistemic objects:

| Claim-ID | Source | Unit of measure | Level of analysis |
|---|---|---|---|
| audio_529 | Ruslan voice memo 24.04.2026 02:48 | Personal income of ICP ($1M+/yr) | Client wealth profile |
| audio_470 | Ruslan voice memo (17.04.2026 context) | Business revenue of client company ($20-50K/month = $240-600K/yr) | Company revenue bracket |
| audio_452 | Ruslan voice memo 15.04.2026 | Ruslan's operational hourly economics (€150/hr × 4 hrs = €600/day) | Ruslan delivery unit |

The critical move: audio_470's «$20-50K/month» is **company monthly revenue** of the client
business — it describes the Startupper ICP bracket (digital business generating $240-600K/yr),
not the client's personal income. This reading is supported by the task context
[src:swarm/wiki/tasks/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25/intake.md#§6] and
consistent with L6's archetype table where Startupper = «$50K-$500K/yr revenue»
[src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]. Personal income of the Startupper may be
50-70% of that revenue figure, not the revenue itself.

L6 qualitative resolution (acked 2026-04-25 01:00 CET): payment-ability filter ($5K/mo OR $10K
one-shot) and P1A/P1B split are binding constraints that already resolve the tension
qualitatively. L7 §5 adds the **quantitative income-floor layer** required for unit-econ
modelling in §3 (LTV assumptions) and §11 (concentration risk register). The L6 acked filter is
NOT overridden; this section adds resolution granularity inside the acked framework.
[src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]

**Acceptance predicate for this section:**
All income-floor claims carry explicit falsifiers AND unit-of-measure labels (personal income vs
business revenue vs deployment budget vs Ruslan hourly unit); the миллионер-tier classification
(Phase-1 P1B referral-only vs Phase-2+ aspirational) is resolved as a binary verdict with
F-G-R triple; the income-floor master table covers all 4 Phase-1 archetypes × 3 phases × 4
pricing tiers; zero claims conflate business revenue with personal income.


## §5.1 Three Source Claims Decomposed

### Claim A — audio_529: «Jetix целится на миллионеров $1M+/year»

**Verbatim context (24.04.2026 02:48 CET, task #471 in review_2026-04-24):** Ruslan is
describing the ICP for clear targeting. The framing is aspirational — the миллионер-tier
($1M+/yr personal income or personal net-worth-generating annual draw) as the premium buyer
archetype. [src:reports/review_2026-04-24.md#row-471]

**Epistemic status:**
- F: F2 (voice memo aspiration; not yet grounded in Phase-1 empirical data)
- ClaimScope: Describes an ICP archetype that EXISTS and PASSES the payment filter easily;
  does NOT prescribe active outreach channel or Phase-1 primary segment
- R: refuted if the миллионер-tier segment proves unreachable via cold outreach in Phase-1;
  accepted if Phase-1 миллионер clients consistently arrive via warm referral (P1B channel)

**Anti-scope of Claim A:** The statement «целится на» does not imply «actively cold-outreach
to». Targeting an income tier as a desired archetype is compatible with reaching that tier
exclusively via referral. The claim is about client quality, not acquisition channel.


### Claim B — audio_470: «клиенты $20-50K/мес ($240-600K/year)»

**Verbatim context (17.04.2026 04:44, task #390 in review_2026-04-24):** Ruslan is calculating
optimal earnings scenarios and client brackets for AI consulting.
[src:reports/review_2026-04-24.md#row-390]

**Critical unit-of-measure resolution:** The $20-50K/month figure is the **client company's
monthly revenue**, not the client owner's personal monthly income. This reading is corroborated
by:

1. L6 §2.1 Startupper archetype profile: «annual revenue $50K-$500K/yr»
   [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1] — the $240-600K/yr bracket of audio_470
   maps directly onto the upper half of the Startupper revenue range.
2. L6 §2.1 Mittelstand archetype: «€1M-€50M company» revenue — audio_470 describes the
   entry-level Startupper, not Mittelstand (whose revenue starts at €1M, well above the $240-600K
   bracket). This confirms two distinct client cohorts.
3. L5 §3.1 Archetype B Startupper pricing: «$50K-$500K/yr revenue; $10K one-shot filter maps
   to ≈€9.3K ceiling» [src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.1]

**Epistemic status:**
- F: F4 (cross-validated across L6 §2.1 Startupper table + L5 §3.1 pricing + intake §6 context)
- ClaimScope: Startupper ICP (English-speaking infobiz digital business); NOT Mittelstand
  (different revenue bracket); NOT personal income of the owner
- R: refuted if audio_470 context is clarified by Ruslan as personal income framing; accepted
  if company revenue framing holds across subsequent client qualification calls


### Claim C — audio_452: «150 евро × 4 часа = 600 кэшфлоу»

**Verbatim context (15.04.2026 02:33, row #7 in insights section, review_2026-04-24):**
«AI-консалтинг может стать одним из первых направлений для заработка — использовать AI для
трекинга, менеджмента и других задач за 50-150 евро в час с генерированием до 600 евро
кэшфлоу в день при работе 4 часа»
[src:reports/review_2026-04-24.md#row-7-insights]

**Epistemic status:**
- F: F5 (anchored to Ruslan's declared rate €150/hr; confirmed as operational anchor across
  L5 §2.1 pricing rationale and CC-1 revenue-mix)
  [src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.0]
- ClaimScope: Ruslan's delivery unit economics at the Phase-A floor; 4-hour workday as
  operational minimum floor, NOT as capacity ceiling
- R: refuted if Ruslan's effective hourly falls below €130/hr in first 5 engagements;
  accepted if first 5 paying engagements close at ≥€130/hr effective rate

**Key separation:** audio_452 describes Ruslan's production side (supplier economics). It says
nothing about client income or client ability to pay. A client paying €5K/mo for a retainer
is implicitly endorsing 33+ hours of Ruslan's €150/hr capacity per month — but the client's
own income is a separate variable entirely.


## §5.2 L6 Partial Resolution Acknowledged

L6 community deep-dive (acked 2026-04-25 01:00 CET) resolved the qualitative dimension:
payment-ability filter (≥$5K/mo recurring OR ≥$10K one-shot) is the operative gate —
not income-tier. The expanded Tier-1 includes Startupper, High-earner, and Mittelstand; the
P1A/P1B sub-prioritization discipline (P1A = Mittelstand + Startupper cold outreach; P1B =
High-earners + миллионеры via referral only) is binding.
[src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]

L7 §5 does not re-litigate these acked decisions. It adds three quantitative outputs that L6
deliberately left as placeholders:

1. **Income-floor for P1A active outreach** — what minimum company revenue AND owner personal
   income signals payment-ability gate clearance with ≥80% probability.
2. **Income-ceiling + channel logic for P1B** — what segment and channel triggers a
   миллионер-tier engagement without violating Ruslan bandwidth-discipline.
3. **Engagement-value compatibility matrix** — which pricing tiers from §2 are affordable by
   which archetype at which phase.


## §5.3 Phase-1 P1A Active Cold Outreach — Income Floor per Archetype

P1A = active cold outreach. Target archetypes: **Operator-Founder-CEO (Mittelstand)** and
**Startupper (English-speaking infobiz)**. [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]

### Operator-Founder-CEO (Mittelstand)

The Mittelstand ICP is an owner-operator of a DACH-region company with:

- **Company revenue:** €1M–€50M (per L6 §2.1 Archetype C table)
  [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]
- **Owner personal annual draw (typical):** €100K–€500K/yr for owner-operators of €1M-€10M
  companies; €500K-€2M+ for €10M-€50M companies (Mittelstand ownership is typically 80-100%
  held by founder, so revenue surplus converts at 15-30% to personal compensation)
- **Deployable strategic budget (annual):** typically 1-3% of company revenue
  - €1M company: €10K-€30K/yr strategic budget
  - €5M company: €50K-€150K/yr strategic budget
  - €10M+ company: €100K-€300K/yr strategic budget
- **Feasible Jetix engagement (§2 pricing reference):** €5K-€18K per engagement (Direction 1
  Path B default: €3K onboarding + €15K/yr license = €18K yr1)
  [src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.3.1]

**Income-floor claim for Mittelstand P1A:**

Company revenue ≥€1M/yr (=owner annual draw likely ≥€100K) with a deployable strategic budget
≥€10K/yr is the minimum viable floor. Below €1M company revenue, the €5K-€18K Jetix engagement
represents >1.5% of annual revenue — a non-trivial allocation that rarely clears internal
approvals without exceptional ROI proof first.

- F: F4 (arithmetic-grounded: 1-3% strategic budget of €1M company = €10-30K/yr; €5K
  engagement = 17-50% of annual budget floor — feasible at upper end only; €5M company
  budget = €50-150K/yr; €5K engagement = 3-10% — comfortable; €18K engagement = 12-36% —
  requires ROI justification but feasible)
- ClaimScope: DACH Mittelstand owner-operators; does NOT apply to corporate middle-managers
  (no P&L ownership) or sole traders below €500K revenue (payment filter fails)
- R: refuted if Mittelstand prospects below €1M company revenue pass payment filter and close
  at listed tier pricing in first 3 attempts; accepted if ≥80% of qualified Mittelstand leads
  show ≥€1M company revenue in discovery Q6 (monthly revenue/budget question)

### Startupper (English-speaking infobiz)

The Startupper ICP is an English-speaking digital business founder with:

- **Company revenue:** $50K–$500K/yr (audio_470 bracket $240-600K/yr = upper half of this
  range) [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]
- **Owner personal income:** typically 60-80% of company revenue for solo/micro-team operators;
  roughly $30K-$400K/yr personal
- **Deployable strategic budget:** more variable than Mittelstand; digital business operators
  often spend 5-15% of revenue on tools + coaching + strategic services (higher % than
  traditional Mittelstand due to lean cost structure)
  - $100K company: $5K-$15K/yr strategic budget — tight for recurring retainer
  - $250K company: $12.5K-$37.5K/yr — viable for €5K/mo retainer at upper range
  - $500K company: $25K-$75K/yr — comfortable for €5K/mo retainer
- **Feasible Jetix engagement (§2 pricing):** €500-€5K (Direction 1 Startupper package);
  Продюсерский центр Pilot €2K-€3K/mo or Standard €4K-€6K/mo
  [src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.1]

**Income-floor claim for Startupper P1A:**

Company revenue ≥$100K/yr (personal income ≥$50K-$80K/yr) with clear signs of audience
monetization is the minimum entry signal. At $100K revenue, a $5K engagement is 5% of annual
revenue — viable for a motivated Startupper who sees ROI. For recurring €4K+/mo retainer,
company revenue ≥$250K/yr is a practical floor.

- F: F4 (analogical from digital business budget norms + L6 payment-filter arithmetic; $5K
  one-shot at $100K company revenue = 5% of revenue; standard B2B threshold for single-vendor
  spend without board approval is typically 3-10% of annual revenue for services)
- ClaimScope: English-speaking infobiz digital operators; does NOT apply to traditional SMBs
  with physical cost structures where 5% of revenue on a single service vendor is very high
- R: refuted if Startuppers below $100K/yr revenue consistently pass discovery Q6 and Q7
  (budget questions) and close; accepted if ≥80% of qualified Startupper leads show ≥$100K/yr
  company revenue in discovery qualification


## §5.4 Phase-1 P1B Opportunistic Referral — Ceiling and Channel Logic

P1B = opportunistic referral. Target archetypes: **High-earner ($100K-$150K+/yr personal)**
and **Миллионер ($1M+/yr personal)**. These arrive inbound — not via active outreach.
[src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]

### High-earner professional ($100K-$150K+/yr personal)

High-earner professionals (specialist consultants, senior attorneys, high-revenue freelancers,
successful bloggers with monetized audiences) have personal income as the primary signal because
their businesses are often solo or micro-team structures where revenue ≈ personal draw.

- **Payment-filter clearance:** $10K one-shot is 7-10% of personal annual income at $100-150K
  — significant but manageable for someone with stable high income and clear ROI framing
- **Feasible engagement:** Direction 1 productized engagement €5K-€10K; Продюсерский центр
  Standard tier €4K-€6K/mo for 3 months = €12K-€18K commitment
- **Channel:** referral-primary; warm intro from existing network; LinkedIn engagement
  (not cold DM to cold account)

**No explicit ceiling for P1B.** Any referral-converted High-earner who passes D22 and payment
filter is a Phase-1 client. The ceiling is Ruslan's bandwidth, not the segment's income:
with 20+ billable hours/week already committed to P1A (CC-1 math), P1B engagements must fit
within residual capacity.

- F: F4 (bandwidth-constraint arithmetic: CC-1 requires 233 hours across H1 2026 ≈ 18-19
  hrs/week; Ruslan's capacity ≈ 30-35 hrs/week total; residual for P1B ≈ 11-16 hrs/week;
  sufficient for 1-2 P1B clients simultaneously at €5K-€10K engagement each)
  [src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.12]
- ClaimScope: Phase-1 bandwidth ceiling; relaxes at G2 when first contractor hired
- R: refuted if High-earner P1B clients consistently consume >20 hrs/engagement (eating into
  P1A CC-1 hours); accepted if P1B engagements remain at ≤15 hrs average

### Миллионер ($1M+/yr personal)

Миллионер-tier clients have annual personal income or capital draw ≥$1M. They trivially pass the
payment filter. Their buyer psychology differs from all other segments: they optimize for
asymmetric upside («насколько умножает мои активы»), not for cost savings or efficiency.
[src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1 Category A]

**Phase-1 channel constraint — critical finding:**

Cold conversion rate for $1M+ ICP via unsolicited outreach approaches zero. Multiple independent
reasons converge (Munger lollapalooza, P4):

1. **Trust barrier (naval specific-knowledge filter, P10):** Миллионеры hire consultants
   through networks of vetted referrals, not via LinkedIn DMs. Their decision process involves
   multiple touchpoints and proof of track record. Phase-1 Ruslan has zero published track record.
2. **Resource mismatch (Stoic dichotomy of control, P5 applicable):** Engaging a миллионер
   client properly requires €20K-€50K/mo retainer pricing (per D-price-1 in §2.13). At that
   pricing, the engagement scope, complexity, and stakeholder management volume exceeds
   Phase-1 solo-Ruslan capacity without degradation.
   [src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.13]
3. **Opportunity cost (Koen sotam, P6):** Active outreach to $1M+ ICP consumes the same
   calendar time as outreach to Mittelstand/Startupper but with near-zero conversion probability.
   The state-of-the-art outreach method for this segment is warm intro, not cold DM.

**Verdict: Миллионер-tier = Phase-1 P1B referral-only segment, NOT active cold-outreach target.**

- F: F3 (substantive with evidence — L6 acked + resource-constraint reasoning + cold-conversion
  near-zero for $1M+ ICP without warm intro, consistent with L6 §2.1 channel guidance for
  миллионеры: «cold к $1M+ segment без warm intro = низкая конверсия»)
  [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]
- ClaimScope: Phase-1 solo-Ruslan bandwidth; cold-outreach channel; fails when warm referral
  arrives organically — then миллионер becomes viable P1B client
- R: refuted if Ruslan closes 2+ миллионер-tier contracts via active cold outreach in
  Q1-Q2 2026 (currently zero empirical basis for cold conversion); accepted if 100% of
  Phase-1 миллионер clients arrive via referral (predicted)

**Phase-1 миллионер P1B engagement ceiling:** €20K single engagement or €5K-€10K/mo
3-month retainer are feasible as P1B when a referral materializes. Not pre-sized in Phase-1
outreach templates. Treated as AWAITING-APPROVAL HITL packet per D-price-1 dissent when
first миллионер referral arrives.
[src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.13]


## §5.5 Миллионер-Tier Classification — Definitive Verdict

**Verdict (binary):** Миллионер-tier ($1M+/yr) is a **real Phase-1 P1B referral-only segment**,
NOT a Phase-1 active cold-outreach target, and IS a Phase-2+ aspirational priority segment.

Three sub-claims, each with F-G-R:

**Sub-claim 5.5.1 — Real segment (not fiction):**
- Claim: Миллионеры exist as a client archetype and pass all filters (payment, D22, upward-direction).
- F: F5 (definitionally true: if personal income ≥$1M/yr, payment filter ≥$5K/mo is trivially met;
  D22 startupper-mindset and upward-direction are behavioral filters that many $1M+ entrepreneurs
  pass; no structural exclusion)
- ClaimScope: archetype exists; individual qualification via D22 still required
- R: unfalsifiable in general (some миллионеры pass D22, some do not); falsifier at individual
  level = failing D22 questions Q2 (AI азарт), Q4 (adequate), Q5 (upward-direction)

**Sub-claim 5.5.2 — Phase-1 P1B referral-only (not cold-outreach):**
- Claim: Active outreach to миллионер-tier in Phase-1 is a resource misallocation given near-zero
  cold conversion and bandwidth constraint.
- F: F3 (L6 channel guidance + bandwidth-discipline argument; empirically unvalidated Phase-1
  since no Phase-1 outreach data yet exists)
- ClaimScope: Phase-1 solo; changes at G2 when track record and team exist
- R: refuted if first 2 миллионер cold outreach attempts convert within Phase-1; accepted if
  all Phase-1 миллионер clients arrive via P1B channel at end of H1 2026

**Sub-claim 5.5.3 — Phase-2+ aspirational (structurally feasible):**
- Claim: As Alliance forms (G2-G3), USB-C productization stabilizes (G2), and team hires (G2-G3),
  миллионер-tier becomes the primary premium client archetype with retainers €20K-€50K/mo.
- F: F4 (L6 §2.1 A miллионер category explicitly identified as Phase-2+ priority via warm
  networks: YPO/EO/Tiger 21; structural feasibility requires track record + Alliance credibility
  + team capacity — all G2+ conditions; analogical from consultancies: McKinsey and equivalents
  take 5-10 years to build the trust capital to command $100K+ monthly retainers)
  [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]
- ClaimScope: G2+ conditions required; fails if Alliance does not form or USB-C productization
  stalls
- R: refuted if first миллионер engagement at €20K+/mo closes in Phase-1; accepted if
  миллионер-tier retainers first appear in Phase-2 (post-€200K gate) engagement logs


## §5.6 Mittelstand €5M Revenue Company — Budget Feasibility Quantified

The Mittelstand reality check requires explicit arithmetic, not handwaving.
[src:swarm/wiki/tasks/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25/intake.md#§6]

**Scenario: owner of €5M/yr revenue Mittelstand company.**

| Variable | Value | Derivation |
|---|---|---|
| Company annual revenue | €5M/yr | Input scenario |
| Typical owner personal draw | €200K-€500K/yr | 4-10% of revenue; Mittelstand owner compensation norms (German GmbH Gesellschafter-Geschäftsführer) |
| Deployable strategic budget | €50K-€150K/yr | 1-3% of revenue; conservative for DACH Mittelstand |
| Jetix AI Consulting retainer (§2 standard) | €5K/mo = €60K/yr | Direction 1 productized; within 1.2% of revenue |
| USB-C Path B (yr1 total) | €18K/yr | €3K onboarding + €15K annual license |
| Retainer as % of strategic budget | 40-120% | Depends on budget size and competing priorities |
| ROI threshold to justify allocation | 30-90 day productivity lift documented | Standard Mittelstand CFO requirement for non-capital expenditure |

**Feasibility verdict:**

€5K/mo retainer = €60K/yr = **1.2% of €5M revenue** — structurally feasible IF:
(a) ROI is demonstrable within 30-90 days, AND
(b) the €5K/mo retainer competes with ≤3 other strategic priorities in that budget year.

The 30-90 day ROI threshold is achievable via knowledge-work productivity lift. A Mittelstand
company with €5M revenue typically has €1M-€3M in knowledge-worker salary cost (20-60% of
revenue at 10-30 employees). A 10% productivity lift on knowledge work = €100K-€300K annual
value. Jetix retainer ROI at this scale = 167% to 500% within 12 months on the productivity
dimension alone.

- F: F4 (arithmetic grounded; knowledge-worker cost % of revenue from DACH SMB benchmarks;
  10% productivity lift is conservative for AI-augmented knowledge work — actual gains in
  early AI adopters reported at 20-40% on specific task types; ROI multiple deliberately
  conservative to survive CFO scrutiny)
- ClaimScope: €5M revenue Mittelstand with ≥10 knowledge workers; does NOT apply to
  manufacturing-heavy companies where knowledge-worker cost is <20% of revenue (ROI case weaker)
- R: refuted if first Mittelstand client at €5K/mo fails to demonstrate measurable
  productivity lift within 90 days of engagement; accepted if ≥2 of first 3 Mittelstand
  clients report positive ROI statement within 90 days

**Pragmatic pricing anchor for Mittelstand by revenue tier:**

| Company revenue | Feasible Jetix engagement | Strategic budget estimate | Feasibility gate |
|---|---|---|---|
| €500K-€1M | €2K-€5K one-shot only | €5K-€30K/yr | CONDITIONAL — one-shot only; no recurring |
| €1M-€5M | €5K-€18K engagement; €2K-€5K/mo retainer | €10K-€150K/yr | YES — with 30-day ROI demonstration |
| €5M-€10M | €5K-€10K/mo retainer; Path B €18K/yr | €50K-€300K/yr | YES — comfortable |
| €10M-€50M | Path C €30K-€45K/yr; €10K-€20K/mo | €100K-€1.5M/yr | YES — Path C enterprise override trigger |


## §5.7 Reconciliation with §2 Pricing Tiers — Which Clients Afford Which Tier

Per-direction compatibility with Phase-1 archetypes:
[src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.1-§2.7]

**Direction 1 (AI Consulting) — floor to standard tier €500-€10K engagement:**
- Startupper ($100K-$500K/yr revenue): YES for Starter €500-€800 and productized €5K; CONDITIONAL
  for retainer €1K-€2K/mo (requires $250K+ company revenue as noted in §5.3)
- Mittelstand (€1M-€10M revenue): YES for productized €5K-€10K and retainer €1K-€2K/mo
- High-earner P1B: YES — $10K engagement is 7-10% annual income, feasible
- Миллионер P1B: YES — trivially affordable; engagement value below aspirational tier but
  available as Phase-1 P1B entry point

**Direction 2 (Продюсерский центр) — Pilot €2K-€3K/mo, Standard €4K-€6K/mo, Premium €7K-€10K/mo:**
- Блогер/Teacher archetype (5K+ audience, monetized): Pilot YES at $100K+ revenue; Standard
  CONDITIONAL at $250K+ revenue; Premium NO in Phase-1 (requires G2 contractor hire for delivery)
- Startupper with content: same as Блогер/Teacher
- Mittelstand: NOT primary target for Продюсерский центр (content production model misaligned
  with B2B manufacturing / professional services ICP)
- Миллионер P1B: Premium YES if referral delivers — but bandwidth constraint applies

**Direction 3 (USB-C Path B) — €3K onboarding + €15K/yr = €18K yr1:**
- Startupper: CONDITIONAL — requires $250K+ revenue and technical team for installation
- Mittelstand (€1M+): YES — primary target; 1.2-1.8% of revenue at €1M company
- High-earner solo: NO — no company IT infrastructure for Path B installation
- Миллионер P1B with company (€10M+): Path C enterprise override (≥€30K); Path B is too
  small for this segment

**Direction 7 (Educational cohort €5K-€8K/learner per L7 arithmetic floor):**
- All Phase-1 professional archetypes: CONDITIONAL — €5K one-time is affordable at $100K+
  personal income; cohort is Phase-2+ (G2→G3)
- Блогер/Teacher: YES if payment filter passes

**Directions 4, 5, 6 (Platform, Network, SaaS — Phase-3 or Phase-2+ tiers):**
- Not applicable for Phase-1 active engagement; mentioned for completeness


## §5.8 Income-Floor Master Table — Archetype × Phase × Pricing-Tier Compatibility

Legend: YES = accessible at listed tier without special conditions; CONDITIONAL = accessible if
stated qualifier met; NO = structurally inaccessible at this phase; UNLOCKS@G2 = becomes
accessible when G2 (€200K gate) conditions met

| Archetype | Phase | Floor tier (€500-€2K) | Standard tier (€2K-€5K/mo or €5K-€10K/eng) | Premium tier (€7K-€10K/mo or €18K-€45K/yr) | Enterprise/aspirational (€20K-€50K/mo) |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| **Startupper** ($50-$250K/yr revenue) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | CONDITIONAL ($250K+/yr) | NO | NO |
| **Startupper** ($250K-$500K/yr revenue) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | YES | CONDITIONAL (G2 contractor needed for delivery) | NO |
| **Startupper** | Phase-2 (G2+) | YES | YES | YES | CONDITIONAL (exceptional) |
| **Блогер/Teacher** (5K+ audience, $50-$150K/yr) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | CONDITIONAL | NO | NO |
| **Блогер/Teacher** (monetized, $150K-$500K/yr) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | YES | CONDITIONAL (G2 needed) | NO |
| **Блогер/Teacher** | Phase-2 (G2+) | YES | YES | YES | CONDITIONAL |
| **Operator-Founder-CEO** Mittelstand (€500K-€1M revenue) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | CONDITIONAL (one-shot only) | NO | NO |
| **Operator-Founder-CEO** Mittelstand (€1M-€5M revenue) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | YES (Path B €18K/yr) | CONDITIONAL (Path C requires >€10M) | NO |
| **Operator-Founder-CEO** Mittelstand (€5M-€50M revenue) | Phase-1 P1A | YES | YES | YES (Path C at €10M+) | UNLOCKS@G2 |
| **Operator-Founder-CEO** | Phase-2 (G2+) | YES | YES | YES | YES (Alliance + track record) |
| **High-earner professional** ($100K-$150K+/yr personal) | Phase-1 P1B | YES | YES (one-shot) | CONDITIONAL (3-month retainer at $150K+) | NO |
| **High-earner professional** | Phase-2 (G2+) | YES | YES | YES | CONDITIONAL |
| **Миллионер** ($1M+/yr personal) P1B referral | Phase-1 P1B only | YES | YES | YES | CONDITIONAL (bandwidth + track record) |
| **Миллионер** | Phase-2 (G2+) aspirational | YES | YES | YES | YES (primary target) |

**Reading guide for the table:**
- Phase-1 P1A = active cold outreach segment; floor is the minimum viable entry point
- Phase-1 P1B = referral-only; no active channel constraint; engagement size limited by
  Ruslan bandwidth, not client affordability
- Phase-2 unlocks reflect: (a) first contractor hire; (b) track record enabling premium
  pricing justification; (c) Alliance structure enabling enterprise-tier confidence


## §5.9 Preserved Dissent — Aspirational vs Floor

**Dissent preserved (D-phil-§5-1):**

- **Position A (aspirational):** Ruslan's audio_529 frames Jetix as targeting миллионеры
  from the start. The company's $1T trajectory requires the methodology to work for the
  highest-value clients from Day 1 as proof of concept. Pricing and channel should be set
  for миллионер-tier, not adjusted downward for Phase-1 operational convenience.
  - F: F2; ClaimScope: aspirational long-horizon; R: validated if Phase-1 first clients
    include миллионер-tier at aspirational pricing without cold-outreach

- **Position B (philosopher-expert verdict):** Phase-1 P1A active outreach sized to
  Mittelstand + Startupper is the resource-disciplined choice (bandwidth constraint, near-zero
  cold conversion rate for миллионер-tier, L6 acked P1A/P1B split). Aspirational target does
  not imply active outreach channel. [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]
  - F: F3; ClaimScope: Phase-1 solo-Ruslan; R: as stated in §5.5.2

**Reconciliation (per E-5 dissent preservation):** Both positions preserved. They are not
contradictory — they occupy different time-horizons and operational modes. Ruslan strategic
override is possible: if a миллионер referral materializes in Phase-1, engage at aspirational
tier without needing this document's permission. This §5 establishes the ACTIVE OUTREACH
default. The default does not preclude INBOUND exceptions. Brigadier escalates AWAITING-APPROVAL
packet when first миллионер referral arrives for HITL pricing decision.

**Trade-off, not contradiction:** The trade-off is between aspirational signaling (expensive:
low conversion, premium pricing in outreach materials) and operational efficiency (affordable:
high P1A conversion, lower tier pricing in Phase-1 templates). The resolution — P1A outreach
at Mittelstand/Startupper tier + P1B templates at миллионер pricing ready in AWAITING-APPROVAL
— captures both positions.


## §5.10 Cross-Section Reconciliation Note

This section feeds three downstream sections of the canonical LAYER-7 document:

**Feeds §2 pricing (Cell C-01 output):** The income-floor table in §5.8 confirms that §2
pricing tiers are correctly calibrated. Direction 1 productized €5K-€10K is affordable by the
primary P1A archetypes (Mittelstand €1M+, Startupper $250K+). No revision to §2 tiers is
required. The §5.3 floor for recurring retainer (€2K-€5K/mo) aligns with Direction 1 monthly
retainer range €1K-€2K/mo (entry) and Direction 2 Pilot tier €2K-€3K/mo.
[src:swarm/wiki/drafts/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25-investor-integrator-§2-pricing.md#§2.1]

**Feeds §3 unit-econ (LTV assumptions):** The income-floor table provides the revenue-ceiling
proxy for LTV modelling. Startupper at $250K/yr company revenue → deployable Jetix budget
$12.5K-$37.5K/yr → LTV ceiling ≈ $25K-$75K per client over 2-3 year engagement (recurring
retainer + add-ons). Mittelstand at €5M revenue → deployable budget €50K-€150K/yr → LTV
ceiling ≈ €100K-€300K per client over 3-5 year engagement. These LTV assumptions are inputs
for §3, not outputs from §3; §5 owns the income-floor component.

**Feeds §11 risk register (concentration risk):** A single миллионер engagement in Phase-1 at
€20K+/mo represents ≥40% of monthly revenue target (€50K/6 months ≈ €8.3K/month average
needed; миллионер at €20K/mo = 2.4× monthly target). Single-client concentration risk: if this
client churns in Month 3, H1 2026 target fails. Mitigation: no single client should represent
>30% of monthly revenue in Phase-1. This directly argues against активating миллионер-tier as
primary Phase-1 revenue line (even if reachable via P1B referral).

**Anti-scope (what this section does NOT do):**
- Does NOT re-open the L6 payment-ability filter ≥$5K/mo or ≥$10K one-shot (acked, binding)
- Does NOT revise §2 pricing tiers (acked in Cell C-01)
- Does NOT authorize активating миллионер cold-outreach — that would require Ruslan HITL override
- Does NOT provide M&A income profiles (deferred Phase-2+ per Ruslan 25.04 directive)
  [src:decisions/STRATEGIC-INSIGHT-MA-DIRECTION-2026-04-25.md#DEFERRED]
- Does NOT provide a model for corporate middle-manager conversion (anti-ICP, excluded)


## §X Cell C-06 Self-Improvement Notes

### Pattern 1 — Income floor is a three-variable function, not a single number

The operationally useful income floor for client qualification is not «income ≥ $X». It is a
function of three variables that must be evaluated jointly:

```
income_floor = f(
  business_revenue,           -- company annual revenue (or personal if solo operator)
  strategic_budget_rate,      -- % of revenue deployable for strategic services (1-15%)
  engagement_value            -- Jetix price point for the target tier
)

gate_pass = (business_revenue × strategic_budget_rate) ≥ (engagement_value × 1.2)
            -- 1.2 multiplier = 20% margin to account for competing budget priorities
```

A Startupper at $500K/yr with 8% strategic budget rate ($40K/yr deployable) passes the gate for
€5K/mo retainer (€60K/yr ≈ $64K — barely misses). At 10% ($50K/yr), it passes. This means
the same archetype at the same income level may or may not qualify depending on budget allocation
behavior. Discovery qualification must probe the budget-rate variable directly (Q6 monthly
revenue, Q7 «if it costs $10K»), not just income level.

**Compound rule candidate:** «income-floor qualification = 3-variable function (business revenue
+ strategic budget rate + engagement value); qualification gate passes only when product of
first two exceeds engagement value × 1.2; discovery Q6 and Q7 probe all three.»

### Pattern 2 — Unit-of-measure decomposition prevents false contradictions

The audio_529 / audio_470 / audio_452 apparent contradiction dissolves immediately once units
of measure are explicitly declared. Three numbers from three different epistemic registers
(client income archetype / client company revenue / Ruslan delivery unit) cannot contradict
each other because they do not occupy the same variable space. The critic role should
default to unit-of-measure decomposition before declaring any apparent inconsistency a real
contradiction — it may be an AP-PHIL-2 (paradigm conflation) instance rather than a genuine
logical tension.

**Compound rule candidate:** «before escalating an apparent multi-source contradiction, run
unit-of-measure decomposition: declare the unit for each claim; claims from different unit
spaces are not contradictory — they are complementary and must be labeled with their respective
scopes.»

### Pattern 3 — Aspirational target vs acquisition channel are orthogonal dimensions

«Targeting» a segment (audio_529 миллионер framing) and «using cold outreach to acquire» that
segment are two independent variables. A company can target $1M+ income clients exclusively as
its long-horizon ideal while using referral-only acquisition in Phase-1 — these are fully
compatible positions. Conflating «target segment» with «primary acquisition channel» produces
false strategic binaries («do we go after миллионеры or not?») when the real question is
«what channel reaches each segment in each phase?». Philosophy-expert should surface this
orthogonality whenever a claim about target audience is interpreted as a claim about outreach
channel.

**Compound rule candidate:** «target-segment identity (who we want) and acquisition-channel
selection (how we reach them) are orthogonal; a claim about target segment carries no implicit
claim about channel; separate both before evaluating consistency with outreach strategy.»


*Draft complete. Cell C-06 philosophy-expert mode critic. Word count estimate: ~3400 words.
Awaiting brigadier §5.5.5 provenance gate before promotion to canonical
LAYER-7-BUSINESS-TRAJECTORY-DEEP-DIVE.md §5.*

# §6 Revenue Streams Ranking + Portfolio Diversification

> **Cell C-04 — mgmt-expert × integrator.** Этот раздел ранжирует потоки выручки Jetix по фазам (Phase-1, Phase-2, Phase-3+), устанавливает пороги концентрации и описывает диверсификационную логику портфеля в терминах, аналогичных портфельному Sharpe-thinking. Раздел потребляет §2 ценообразования (L7 owner) и §13 evolution из L5 как входные данные — он не пересматривает pricing arithmetic, а использует уже зафиксированные диапазоны как ориентиры структуры потоков. Сноска на §7 cash flow и §11 risk register внутри документа явная.


## §6.0 Фрейминг — что такое revenue stream и почему portfolio matters

**Revenue stream** — это дискретный канал поступления денег, идентифицируемый по паре (продукт/услуга × механика оплаты). Два потока от одного клиента — разные revenue streams, если механика оплаты различается (например: retainer-контракт vs success-fee). Понятие stream принципиально отличается от понятия direction (L5 §2): одно направление (например, AI Consulting) может порождать несколько streams (hourly overflow + productized package + retainer).

**Portfolio** — набор активных revenue streams в текущей фазе. Задача портфеля — не максимизировать один поток, а обеспечить устойчивый совокупный доход через баланс коррелированных и антикоррелированных источников. [src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§1 Plan Overview]

**Concentration risk** — ситуация, при которой один клиент или один stream генерирует долю, достаточную для того, чтобы его потеря угрожала cash-flow всей фазы. Threshold определён в L6 §2.1: **ни один клиент не должен превышать 30% общей фазовой выручки**. [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1] Это операционный закон, а не ориентир.

**Claim §6.0-C1:**
- F: F4 (операционная конвенция, закреплённая в L6 ack)
- ClaimScope: действует для Phase-1 solo-operator; применимость к Phase-3+ multi-BU требует уточнения (threshold может быть тоньше)
- R: опровергается, если единственный крупный клиент не уходит в Phase-1 (risk never materalised) — но это ex-post; accepted как architecture constraint a priori


## §6.1 Phase-1 (€0 → €50K Q2 2026) — ранжирование потоков

### Первичные потоки (≥40% каждый)

**Phase-1 Revenue Mix (ack'd CC-1 per KM-Mat-MVP investor audit):**

| Stream | Объём | Цена | Выручка Q1+Q2 |
|---|---|---|---|
| Productized contracts (Path-B) | 4 contract-quarters (2 × 2Q) | €7 500/contract-quarter | €30 000 |
| Hourly consulting (4-pack "конкретная помощь" + discovery) | 233 часа | €150/час [audio_452] | €35 000 |
| **Итого (gate: €50K)** | | | **€65 000 (~30% margin)** |

[src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§3.1.1]

**AI Consulting (productized contracts + hourly overflow) — ~100% Phase-1 cash-flow в узком смысле.** Подробнее: productized sub-stream даёт €30K (~46% от €65K ceiling), hourly sub-stream — €35K (~54%). Оба принадлежат одному направлению (Direction 1 — AI Consulting), но имеют разные mechanics и разный операционный риск:

- **Productized contracts (Path-B default per L5 Q1 ack):** GM 70.7% [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#frontmatter brigadier_top5_ack_recommendations]. Риск: медленный sales cycle (6–12 недель). Защита: если 2 контракта/квартал не закрываются, весь €30K plan рушится — hourly становится критическим.
- **Hourly consulting:** более ликвидный, быстрее конвертируется из discovery-звонков. Риск: hours-ceiling (Ruslan — единственный deliverer; физически ограничен ~20 часов/неделю billable). [src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§3.1.1 implication: ≥20 hours/week]

**Продюсерский центр (pilot) — co-primary, внутри Phase-1 ceiling.** Pilot format: 1-2 клиента × retainer €4K/мес × 6 мес ≈ €24K потенциал. Перекрывается с consulting ICP (Блогер + Startupper — один outreach motion приводит к обоим). [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1 Sub-prioritization] Важно: Продюсерский центр **входит** в общий €65K ceiling как вторая активная линия — не добавляется к ней. При расчёте доли в портфеле нужно рассматривать суммарно.

**Claim §6.1-C1 (Phase-1 primary streams):**
- F: F4 (операционная конвенция, закреплённая в CC-1 ack)
- ClaimScope: действует для Phase-1 Q1+Q2 2026 solo-operator; не действует без ≥20 часов/неделю billable capacity
- R: опровергается, если productized contract pipeline < 2/квартал AND hourly < 15 часов/неделю устойчиво → €50K gate не достигается

### Вторичные потоки (5–20% Phase-1)

**Matchmaker incidental:** €0 прямого revenue в Phase-1. Функция: leverage для acquisition consulting-клиентов (Ruslan вручную коннектирует людей → trust building → referrals → consulting leads). [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.5 P1B opportunistic referral] Считается secondary lever, не revenue stream в Phase-1.

**USB-C early-access (P1B opportunistic):** первый клиент возможен как opportunistic, не как планируемый target. Path-B unit economics при случайном первом клиенте: €3K-€10K/мес engagement. Не включается в €65K baseline — учитывается как upside buffer.

**Hourly overflow (уже в primary):** почасовые discovery-сессии уже захвачены в основном hourly-stream. Дублирования нет.

### Concentration thresholds — Phase-1

**Правило №1 (L6 §2.1 verbatim):** ни один клиент > 30% общей Phase-1 выручки. При target €50K это означает: ни один клиент > €15K суммарно за Phase-1. [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1]

**Следствие (количественное):** при средней величине контракта ~€7.5K/квартал (Path-B), минимальный «безопасный» портфель требует ≥4-5 активных клиентов. Один productized contract + остальное hourly = 1 клиент potentially >30% → структурный риск концентрации. Решение: диверсифицировать hourly across 3-5 clients, а не одним большим engagement.

**Правило №2 (mgmt-inferred от структуры):** ни один direction > 70% выручки в Phase-1. Поскольку оба primary (consulting + producer) активны с P1A outreach, target — 45-55% balance между ними. Если producer pilot не стартует в Q1 → consulting = 100% → direction-concentration risk.

**Claim §6.1-C2 (concentration thresholds):**
- F: F4 (L6 §2.1 ack'd + mgmt-inferred arithmetic)
- ClaimScope: Phase-1 solo-operator €50K gate; threshold 30% = hard rule из L6
- R: опровергается только если Ruslan явно пересматривает L6 §2.1 в HITL-гейте; принят как binding constraint


## §6.2 Phase-2 (€50K → €200K → €1M) — ранжирование потоков

### Gate 1 (€50K → €200K) — validation window

**Primary: AI Consulting (declining %)** остаётся крупнейшим stream, но его доля снижается по мере появления новых потоков. Consulting эволюционирует: hourly → retainer → productized managed service (D18 productization path). [src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§4.1]

**Primary: Продюсерский центр (growing %)** становится main revenue driver начала Phase-2 ([src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§5.5]): productized fully (D18). 1-2 → 3-5 retainer clients at €4K-€8K/мес = €12K-€40K/мес ceiling. По мере появления hire #1 (sales) продажи ускоряются.

**Новые streams, запускаемые в Phase-2:**

| Stream | Механика | Примерный размер (placeholder) | Gate |
|---|---|---|---|
| Subscription — Secure Network складчина | Subscriptions €200-€500/мес × growing membership | Starts post-G3 (€1M) — BUILIDING at G2 | G2→G3 architecture design, G3 launch |
| Path A/B/C USB-C contracts | Retainer €3K-€20K/мес per Path | First client G1→G2 transition opportunistic; productized at G2 | G1→G2 |
| Educational cohort | €50K per cohort (€3K-€8K × 15-20 learners), 1-2 cohorts/quarter at G2→G3 | Target: €50K/cohort × 2/quarter = €100K/quarter | G2→G3 (NPS>40 + margin>€3K/learner gate) |
| Matchmaker AI-smoothed fees | €500-€2K per match | Small but growing; Phase-2 product form at G2 | G1→G2 AI-smoothed |

[src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§5.5; decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.5; swarm/wiki/tasks/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25/intake.md#§3]

**Важная оговорка — Secure Network:** согласно L5 §2.5 и JETIX-PLAN §4.4, Secure Network build starts после €200K validation gate. Subscribe revenue появляется **только post-G3** (€1M). В окне G2 (€50K-€200K) это invite-list, не revenue stream. [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.5 P1B]

### Concentration thresholds — Phase-2

- Ни один клиент > 25% total Phase-2 revenue
- Ни один direction > 50% total revenue к G2 (€200K)
- Ни один direction > 40% total revenue к G3 (€1M)

По мере появления educational cohort + matchmaker fees + USB-C contracts, consulting+producer как пара должна опуститься ниже 50% совокупной выручки к концу Phase-2.

**Claim §6.2-C1 (Phase-2 new streams onboarding):**
- F: F3 (паттерн наблюдаемый в аналогичных consulting-to-platform transitions; не верифицирован на Jetix Phase-1 данных)
- ClaimScope: Phase-2 solo→managed-team; holds for consulting-motion с productization (D18); NOT valid для pure-SaaS transition (другая динамика)
- R: опровергается, если educational cohort NPS<40 или margin<€3K/learner после первых 2 cohorts — тогда cohort revenue stream не масштабируется и должен быть tombstone'd per §3.10 Q4 ack


## §6.3 Phase-3+ ($1M → $100M → $1T) — ранжирование потоков

На этом горизонте портфель трансформируется: services-heavy → methodology+subscription+asset-driven.

### Первичные потоки Phase-3+

**Methodology licensing royalties (D27 Fork-and-Merge):** Practitioners (co-consultants, roys) платят за лицензию методологии и участие в Alliance ecosystem. Два ценовых уровня: practitioner €500-€5K/год; co-consultant network revenue-share (% от их выручки, generated через Jetix methodology). D27 fork-and-merge governance: лучшие форки возвращают улучшения upstream → методология улучшается за счёт сети. [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§3.7 Educational + Licensing]

**Secure Network subscription (membership tiers):** Post-G3 launch: €200-€500/мес basic; premium tiers выше. При 1000-5000 members (G4 cardinality per L6 §11): €200K-€2.5M/мес subscription ceiling. [src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§11 Evolution table G4]

**USB-C standard-layer (Alliance dues + Path A managed hosting):** Alliance membership dues (Foundation operating fees); Path A managed hosting subscriptions (enterprise clients, recurring €5K-€20K/мес). По мере роста Alliance — сетевой эффект увеличивает и базу, и ARPU. [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§3.3 USB-C §5 Offer structure]

**Educational license tier:** Methodology repo v1 (Apache 2.0 free → commercial license tier); certified consultant program (Phase-3+, G3→G4); institutional educational licenses (€500-€5K/год). По оценке: 12+ paid cohorts до запуска certification per §3.7 Q5. [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§3.7]

### Вторичные / опциональные потоки Phase-3+

**Token economy (D23 Option B) — IF launched:**  
Per Ruslan Q5 ack (2026-04-25): preserve optionality; retirement clause triggers if consulting/educational/USB-C fund growth without specialist-friction AND MiCA/Howey legally prohibitive. [src:swarm/wiki/tasks/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25/intake.md#§3] Если токен запущен: ecosystem service payments denominated in JCU; specialist compensation; складчина tool-pooling внутри Secure Network. Активация: Phase-3 ($100K self-earned internal utility trigger); public layer Phase-3+ ($100M). НЕ автоматический — retirement clause явный. [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§3.8]

**Claim §6.3-C1 (Token optionality):**
- F: F3 (conditional on regulatory clarity + self-funded growth + specialist-friction materialization)
- ClaimScope: Phase-3+; NOT valid for Phase-1/2; conditional on D23 retirement clause NOT firing
- R: опровергается (token retired), если consulting+educational+USB-C достигают $100M ARR без specialist-compensation friction → D23 deprecation per LOCKS-D23-DEPRECATION

**Holding investment returns (D11 + D19):** Equity в roys; Kelly portfolio multi-roy. Phase-3+ по мере формирования holding structure. [src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§6 Phase 3] Механика: investment-fund philosophy (D11) — Ruslan allocates capital в roys (подтверждённые методологические ответвления); holding returns — dividends/equity appreciation. Timeline: $1M gate (Phase-3 start) → holding structure formalized per JETIX-PLAN §6.

**M&A Advisory (Phase-2+ optionality — brief mention only):**  
Per Ruslan 25.04 directive: деferred to Phase-2+; NOT Phase-1 priority. [src:decisions/STRATEGIC-INSIGHT-MA-DIRECTION-2026-04-25.md#deferred-status-note] Если активирован при €200K validation AND co-founder secured: success-fees €1-2M per Mittelstand mid-market deal (€30-50M EV × 2-4%). Bimodal revenue profile: **€1-2M если mandate closes; €0 если retainer-only без close**. Dedicated deep-dive cycle when Ruslan re-prioritizes.

**Claim §6.3-C2 (M&A optionality):**
- F: F2 (единственный источник — Wall Street research + Ruslan brief verbatim 25.04; no Phase-1 data)
- ClaimScope: Phase-2+ only if co-founder secured + DACH geography active; NOT Phase-1
- R: опровергается (M&A retired), если 6-18 месячный sales cycle делает M&A несовместимым с Phase-2 cash-flow runway; принят как upside optionality item


## §6.4 Diversification Logic — Portfolio Sharpe-Equivalent

Классический Sharpe ratio максимизирует return при заданной волатильности. В отсутствие достаточной Phase-1 статистики прямой расчёт невозможен, но структурная логика применима: **какие потоки коррелируют (падают одновременно), а какие антикоррелируют (стабильны в рецессию)**.

### Correlation matrix (качественная)

**Группа A — проциклические (B2B AI services demand):**
- AI Consulting (productized + hourly)
- Продюсерский центр retainers
- USB-C Integration Services contracts (Path A/B/C)

Корреляция: все три привязаны к discretionary B2B spend. В рецессию Mittelstand сокращает consultancy бюджеты первыми. DACH recession risk 2026-27 (R-15 risk, L7 §11 owner) — прямо ударяет по этой группе. Одновременное снижение всех трёх создаёт worst-case cash-flow gap.

**Группа B — мягко-коррелированные (resilient, но не immune):**
- Educational cohort (demand shifts в рецессию: люди переобучаются)
- Subscription Secure Network (низкий ticket = meньше churn в рецессию чем enterprise contracts)

Эти два потока устойчивы к мягким рецессиям. В глубокой рецессии discretionary learning тоже сжимается, но позже и менее драматично чем B2B services.

**Группа C — антициклические (lagging или counter-cyclical):**
- Methodology licensing royalties (once launched: инфраструктурный тип revenue — платят, пока используют методологию; перестают только при bankcruptcy или смене стека)
- Holding investment returns (диверсифицированы по рояльным портфелям; если Kelly-disciplined — не коррелируют с DACH SMB cycle напрямую)

**Группа D — некоррелированные (own cycle):**
- Token economy (IF launched): crypto market имеет собственный цикл, не коррелирующий с DACH SMB recession. Может быть positive в рецессию (риск-аппетит к альтернативным активам) или negative (risk-off). Не управляемая корреляция — чистая некоррелированность.

**Claim §6.4-C1 (diversification analysis):**
- F: F3 (структурная аналогия с известными паттернами B2B services + SaaS; не эмпирические данные Jetix)
- ClaimScope: holds для DACH market context + solo-founder Phase-1/2; NOT valid для US market где B2B spend менее cyclical чем в Германии
- R: опровергается, если Phase-1 empirical data покажет, что consulting churn в DACH recession < 20% (тогда группа A более stable чем структурно ожидается)

### Diversification targets per phase

| Phase | % Anti-cyclic streams в портфеле | Почему |
|---|---|---|
| Phase-1 | ~0% (no anti-cyclic streams operational yet) | Вынужденно: subscription/licensing не запущены |
| Phase-2 (G2) | 15-25% (subscription early + educational) | Первые anti-cyclic streams появляются |
| Phase-3 (G3) | ≥30% (subscription + educational + licensing early) | Трёхпотоковая база |
| Phase-3+ | ≥40% (full anti-cyclic portfolio operational) | Целевой уровень устойчивости |

**Главный вывод Phase-1/2:** Jetix вынужден оставаться проциклическим на ранних фазах — нет выбора. Единственная защита = **клиентская диверсификация** (concentration threshold <30% per client) и **geographic diversification** (English+US primary, DACH secondary — рецессии не синхронны). [src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§1 Geographic rollout]


## §6.5 Concentration Risk Thresholds per Phase

| Metric | Phase-1 | Phase-2 | Phase-3 | Phase-3+ |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| Single client max | <30% total revenue | <25% total revenue | <15% total revenue | <10% total revenue |
| Single direction max | <70% (consulting+producer pair jointly active) | <50% к G2; <40% к G3 | <35% | <30% |
| Single roy (Phase-3+) | n/a | n/a | <30% roy portfolio | <20% |
| Single stream max (Phase-3+) | n/a | n/a | <35% | <30% |

[src:decisions/LAYER-6-COMMUNITY-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.1 single-client >30% threshold; decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§3.10 exit criteria "portfolio diversified"]

**Phase-3+ balance target:** methodology + subscription + token (if active) + roy returns — равномерное распределение между Группами A, B, C per §6.4.

**Операционное следствие Phase-1:** если к M1.2 (€20K) все деньги получены от одного клиента → триггер для немедленной диверсификации outreach. Это не просто бизнес-риск — это нарушение concentration threshold, который является **acceptance condition** Phase-1 exit criteria.


## §6.6 Phase-1 → Phase-2: Sequencing — как новые потоки onboard'ятся

Новые revenue streams не должны разбавлять Phase-1 capacity. Sequencing следует из D15 (revenue-gated spend) и D18 (productization path):

**Шаг 1 — Secure Network invite-list (G1, €50K):** Не revenue stream — pre-enrollment. Первые 5-20 high-quality contacts. Zero spend. Build в Phase-1 = нет. Revenue = нет. [src:decisions/LAYER-5-PRODUCT-DIRECTIONS-DEEP-DIVE.md#§2.5]

**Шаг 2 — USB-C first client (G1→G2 transition):** Path A/B/C первый contract opportunistic (P1B). Не планируемый outreach target — появляется если consulting engagement естественно растёт до managed-methodology scope. Unlock trigger: первый контракт >€30K+GDPR-audit (Path-C override per L5 Q1). [src:swarm/wiki/tasks/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25/intake.md#§3 L5 acked inputs]

**Шаг 3 — Matchmaker AI-smoothed (G1→G2):** При первом hire (sales), Ruslan передаёт manual matchmaking на AI-smoothed layer. Fees начинают появляться но остаются небольшими (€500-€2K/match). Net-new stream, не замена consulting.

**Шаг 4 — Educational cohort первый (G2→G3):** ТОЛЬКО после Secure Network architecture design завершена. Первый paid cohort = методология достаточно стабильна для обучения. Acceptance gate: NPS>40 + margin>€3K/learner. [src:swarm/wiki/tasks/T-layer-7-business-trajectory-deep-dive-2026-04-25/intake.md#§3]

**Шаг 5 — Secure Network subscription launch (G3, €1M):** Первые subscription revenues. Это архитектурный gate — не раньше €200K validation (D15) и не раньше первого cohort validated. [src:decisions/JETIX-PLAN.md#§5.2]

**Главный принцип sequencing:** каждый новый stream открывается только после того, как предыдущая ступень валидирована и не требует Ruslan'ского full-attention. Иначе — AP-MGMT-4 (scope creep) и риск срыва Phase-1 €50K target.

**Claim §6.6-C1 (sequencing protection):**
- F: F4 (operational convention per D15 revenue-gated + D18 productization path; закреплено в Locks)
- ClaimScope: Phase-1 solo-operator; NOT valid при наличии 5+ team (тогда parallel streams не создают одиночного bottleneck)
- R: опровергается, если появляется inbound demand на новый stream (например клиент сам просит educational content) → тогда opportunistic открытие допустимо, НО requires explicit Ruslan ack (scope gate)


## §6.7 Cross-Section Reconciliation Note

**Dependences on/from other §§ L7:**

- **→ §3 Unit Economics:** pricing arithmetic для каждого stream (hourly €150/hr, Path-B €7.5K/quarter, cohort €50K, subscription €200-€500/мес) является ВХОДОМ из §2 Pricing + §3 Unit Econ. Если §2/§3 изменят ranges → доли портфеля в §6 обновляются пропорционально. Mgmt не пересматривает pricing — consumption only.
- **→ §7 Cash Flow:** Phase-1 cash flow model (monthly Q1-Q2 2026) потребляет revenue-stream timing из §6 (какой stream когда начинает генерировать cash). Разрыв: subscription revenue появляется only post-G3 → в Phase-1 cash model она = €0.
- **→ §11 Risk Register:** concentration risk thresholds (§6.5) питают §11 risk register напрямую: single-client >30% = explicit risk entry. DACH recession (R-15) = demand shock на Группу A (§6.4) = quantified cash-flow impact в §11.
- **→ §13 Evolution Master:** ranking shares per gate (G1→G5) в §13 должны совпадать с §6 фазовой логикой. Если §13 даёт другой ranking order → conflict flag для brigadier.


## §X Cell C-04 Self-Improvement Notes

**Pattern 1 — Concentration threshold → minimum client count formula:**

Phase-1 single-client threshold 30% при target €50K = max €15K per client. При средней величине engagement (Path-B hourly mix: ~€7-10K per client over Phase-1) минимальный безопасный N = ceiling(1/0.30) = **4 clients**. Универсальная формула: N_min = ceiling(1/threshold). При threshold 25% (Phase-2): N_min = 4; при threshold 15% (Phase-3): N_min = 7. Это прямой KPI для outreach velocity: если N_active < N_min → concentration risk.

**Pattern 2 — Anti-cyclic stream onboarding lag:**

Subscription + licensing = anti-cyclic, но оба требуют 12-24 месяцев build time ПОСЛЕ revenue gate. Если DACH recession приходит в 2026-27 (R-15), Jetix встречает её с проциклическим портфелем даже если Phase-1 выполнена. Вывод: anti-cyclic streams не "страховка на Phase-1" — они страховка на Phase-3. Единственная Phase-1/2 защита от recession = geographic diversification (US demand vs DACH demand не синхронны) + клиентская диверсификация (N_min).

**Pattern 3 — Bimodal stream risk:**

M&A success-fees и token revenues — bimodal: либо крупный event (€1-2M сделка; token utility launch), либо €0. Bimodal streams нельзя включать в cash-flow baseline — только в upside scenario. Правило: baseline cash model = только predictable streams (retainer + hourly + subscription + licensing). Bimodal streams входят в "upside sensitivity" расчёт §7, не в base case.
